24:829:60150:15:11:108:504:149:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:related to the original composition. Either assumption captures situations of the following kind: A
24:830:60249:11:11:108:504:138:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:consumer is inclined to buy a good based on superficial information. That said, she is not aware of
24:831:60348:11:11:108:504:127:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:all aspects, such as hidden costs, that could influence her decision. Further, discovering one aspect
24:832:60449:11:0:108:341:116:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:is not necessarily informative about undiscovered aspects.
25:833:60509:0:17:108:503:673:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:of itself, less important. To see this point, let ̃xih= ̃ximfor alliin the first (landlord)
25:834:60600:17:16:108:504:656:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:example above. Increasingmleaves the total payoff, ̃y, unchanged but shrinks every
25:835:60682:16:17:108:503:640:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:component, ̃xim. Crucially, this reduces how much the DM can learn from a given
25:836:60761:17:16:108:219:623:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:number of components.
25:837:60782:16:17:124:504:607:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:Payoff-equivalent variation is thus a means of manipulating the DM’s learning
25:838:60859:17:16:108:504:590:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:process. How the expert uses such means hinges, as before, on the DM’s decision
25:839:60938:16:17:108:503:574:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:rule. If she uses an opt-in rule, the expert wants to help her learn more aboutA.
25:840:61019:17:16:108:504:557:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:He would setN≤2—such that no relevant aspect escapes deliberation—and exert
25:841:61094:16:16:108:503:541:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f4:B:communication effort on all the components. That is, he would simplify the payoff
25:842:61175:16:17:108:255:525:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:structure and strive to explain.
25:843:61207:17:16:124:503:508:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:By contrast, if the DM follows an opt-out rule, the expert wants to do the exact
25:844:61287:16:17:108:504:492:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:opposite. He would increase the number of components, even if it were costly to do
25:845:61369:17:25:108:462:475:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:so, only to thwart learning. Suppose he must payv>0to raiseNby one.
25:846:61436:25:17:108:509:450:119:g_d0_f12:119:g_d0_f5:C:Proposition 4(Complexification).Let ̄α>α∗.Supposeallrelevantcuesaresent
25:847:61507:17:16:108:508:433:119:g_d0_f5:119:g_d0_f5:C:out. Asv→0,theexpertsetsN→+∞,andtheDM’sexpectedutilityfallsto
25:848:61568:16:25:108:136:417:119:g_d0_f13:119:g_d0_f5:C:E( ̃x).
25:849:61575:25:17:124:503:392:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:Asv→0, the expert increasesNsuch that more relevant information escapes
25:850:61646:17:16:108:504:375:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:the DM’s attention, given that she can deliberate on only a limited number of com-
25:851:61728:16:17:108:504:359:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:ponents. At the same time, he disaggregates the payoffto reduce the amount of
25:852:61805:17:16:108:504:342:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:information she can possibly wrest from any given component. In the limit, even
25:853:61884:16:17:108:504:326:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:what she can learn from the components she is capable of studying becomes so trivial
25:854:61968:17:16:108:504:309:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:that it no longer affects her decision: She chooses what she would have chosen with-
25:855:62052:16:16:108:504:293:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:out the information. Intuitively, the expert makes the action unnecessarily complex,
25:856:62136:16:17:108:442:277:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:and thereby succesfully prevents the DM from getting the full picture.
25:857:62206:17:16:124:503:260:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:Complexification thus has the same welfare consequences as inducing information
25:858:62285:16:17:108:504:244:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:overload — it can eradicate all intended welfare gains from mandated information
25:859:62365:17:31:108:414:227:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:provision, even if the mandate prohibits unclear communication.
25:860:62428:31:17:108:504:196:119:g_d0_f12:119:g_d0_f3:B:Complexification in practiceAccording to Edward L. Yingling, president and
25:861:62502:17:16:108:504:179:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:chief executive of the American Bankers Association (ABA), during his first term
25:862:62582:16:17:108:504:163:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:Obama urged credit card companies “to issue asimplecredit card product” (emphasis
25:863:62663:17:16:108:504:146:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:added). A year earlier, after similar comments by Federal Reserve Chairman Ben S.
25:864:62744:16:17:108:504:130:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:Bernanke “that improved disclosures alone cannot solve all of the problems consumers
25:865:62828:17:0:108:504:113:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:face in trying to manage their credit card accounts,” the ABA and other industry
26:866:62910:0:17:108:440:673:119:g_d0_f3:64:g_d0_f6:B:representatives had signaled strong opposition to such interventions.24
26:867:62981:17:16:124:503:656:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:The UK financial regulator, the Financial Services Authority (FSA), is also
26:868:63056:16:24:108:190:640:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:quoted as saying:
26:869:63073:24:16:151:476:616:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:[P]roviders of financial products may gain from the lack of price trans-
26:870:63145:16:17:135:476:600:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:parency about their products. [. . . ] It may be in the provider’s interest
26:871:63220:17:24:135:373:583:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:to increase the complexity of the product charges.
26:872:63270:24:16:108:504:559:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:Other examples of complexification come from the food industry, where legislation
26:873:63351:16:16:108:504:543:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:mandates that all ingredients be listed in a food declaration; however, “incidental
26:874:63434:16:17:108:504:527:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:additives” need not be listed.  This has provided food producers with incentives
26:875:63514:17:16:108:504:510:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:for complexification, most prominently by removing an ingredient that consumers
26:876:63593:16:17:108:504:494:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:may be want to avoid, and replacing it with one or several incidental additives that
26:877:63677:17:16:108:503:477:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:accomplish the same effect in food but that remain invisible (provided each of them
26:878:63760:16:17:108:504:461:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:is included in small enough a quantity). A recent example is Starbuck’s use of a color
26:879:63846:17:16:108:504:444:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:additive derived from the animal world classified as an incidental additive instead of
26:880:63932:16:17:108:504:428:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:an ingredient, which effectively caused a non-vegan product to be labeled vegan and
26:881:64015:17:16:108:504:411:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:caused a stir among vegan consumers.25Similarly, widespread consumer awareness
26:882:64093:16:16:108:504:395:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:of the dangers of BPA has spurred development of a new range of plastic products
26:883:64173:16:17:108:504:379:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:labelled “BPA Free”; however, these products contain BPA replacement substances
26:884:64252:17:16:108:503:362:119:g_d0_f3:64:g_d0_f6:B:that have produced health problems similar to those associated with BPA itself.26
26:885:64333:16:17:108:504:346:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:Clearly, in the absence of mandated disclosure of the ingredients in food, none of
26:886:64415:17:16:108:504:329:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:these complexifications was necessary; in the presence of this disclosure rule, however,
26:887:64503:16:17:108:433:313:119:g_d0_f3:64:g_d0_f6:B:they represented strategic responses on the part of food producers.27
26:888:64572:17:16:124:503:296:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:As opposed to the examples presented in the previous subsection, which showed
26:889:64649:16:16:108:503:280:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:manipulation of the complexity ofinformation, the examples provided here refer to
26:890:64730:16:17:108:503:264:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:manipulation of the complexity of theproductitself.  Whether the complexity of
26:891:64808:17:15:108:504:247:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:information or the complexity of the product itself is involved, the danger is that
26:892:64891:15:15:116:504:232:36:g_d0_f7:80:g_d0_f8:F:24Labaton, Stephen. 2008. “U.S. Seeks New Curbs on Credit-Card Practices,”New York Times,
26:893:64980:15:7:108:387:217:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:May 3, http://www.nytimes.com/2008/05/03/business/03credit.html
26:894:65043:7:15:116:503:210:36:g_d0_f7:80:g_d0_f8:F:25Source: Fortney D. Beware: Starbucks’ Soy Strawberries & Creme Frappuccino Is NOT vegan
26:895:65132:15:11:108:504:195:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:[weblog entry]. This Dish Is Veg (14 Mar 2012). Available: http://goo.gl/kPpj5 [accessed 11 Mar
26:896:65227:11:7:108:132:184:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:2016].
26:897:65233:7:15:116:503:177:36:g_d0_f7:80:g_d0_f8:F:26Source:  LaMotte S. BPA-free plastic alternatives may not be safe as you think (1 Feb
26:898:65320:15:11:108:504:162:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:2016). Available: http://www.cnn.com/2016/02/01/health/bpa-free-alternatives-may-not-be-safe/
26:899:65413:11:7:108:203:151:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:[accessed 11 Mar 2016].
26:900:65436:7:15:116:503:144:36:g_d0_f7:80:g_d0_f8:F:27Bjorkegren(2016) analyzes data from the FDA Food Labeling and Packaging Survey from 1976
26:901:65526:15:11:108:504:129:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:through 2006. He documents rising product complexity in food over this time period, and explains
26:902:65622:11:10:108:504:118:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:how food product design reflects the introduction of various types of labeling regulations with great
26:903:65723:10:0:108:146:108:80:g_d0_f8:80:g_d0_f8:F:precision.
27:904:65735:0:17:108:503:673:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:misguided decisions affect consumers’ risk of getting into debt or of buying food
27:905:65816:17:16:108:267:656:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:products that they wish to avoid.
27:906:65849:16:17:124:503:640:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:However, while complexity of information has a simple legislative recipe man-
27:907:65926:17:16:108:504:623:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:dating that firms provide easy-to-understand information, complexification is much
27:908:66008:16:17:108:504:607:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:harder to address from a legislative perspective. In fact, Proposition4, along with
27:909:66091:17:16:108:504:590:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:the real-world examples of complexification presented in this subsection, underscore
27:910:66175:16:17:108:504:574:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:that even the most elaborate disclosure rule – which specifies exactly how easy-to-
27:911:66258:17:16:108:504:557:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:understand-information should be provided – may be completely ineffective for the
27:912:66339:16:16:108:504:541:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:consumer. This is becauseanyregulation at the communication level proves futile
27:913:66418:16:17:108:503:525:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:if the seller can modify theobjectof communication in a way that makes it intel-
27:914:66498:17:16:108:504:508:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:lectually challenging to grasp, even with all details correctly disclosed. While the
27:915:66582:16:17:108:504:492:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:communication is correct, the matter to be decided becomes too complicated. In
27:916:66660:17:16:108:503:475:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:such a case, to be effective, regulation may have to target the object of communi-
27:917:66742:16:17:108:504:459:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:cation per se, that is, product design. This, as the examples illustrate, is a much
27:918:66825:17:38:108:175:442:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:thornier issue.
27:919:66840:38:27:108:207:404:206:g_d0_f2:206:g_d0_f2:C:4  Conclusion
27:920:66853:27:16:108:504:377:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:Limits on consumer attention limitations give firms incentives to manipulate prospec-
27:921:66938:16:17:108:504:361:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:tive buyers’ allocation of their attention. To the best of my knowledge, this paper
27:922:67021:17:16:108:504:344:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:is the first to model such attention manipulation. In its presence, competitive in-
27:923:67104:16:17:108:504:328:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:formation supply can reduce consumer knowledge by causing information overload.
27:924:67183:17:16:108:504:311:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:Moreover, a single firm subjected to a disclosure mandate may deliberately induce
27:925:67264:16:17:108:504:295:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:information overload to obfuscate financially relevant information, or engage in prod-
27:926:67350:17:16:108:383:278:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:uct complexification to bound consumer financial literacy.
27:927:67408:16:16:124:505:262:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:These findings demonstrate that attention limitations matter crucially for whether
27:928:67490:16:17:108:504:246:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:disclosure regulation improves consumer welfare: Disclosure rules that would improve
27:929:67574:17:16:108:504:229:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:welfare for agents without attention limitations can prove ineffective for consumers
27:930:67658:16:17:108:504:213:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:with limited attention. Obfuscation suggests a role for rules that mandate not only
27:931:67741:17:16:108:504:196:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:the content but also the format of disclosure; however, even rules that mandate dis-
27:932:67825:16:17:108:503:180:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:closure of “easy-to-understand” information are ineffective against complexification,
27:933:67910:17:16:108:336:163:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:which may call for regulation of product design.
27:934:67958:16:17:124:503:147:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:An interesting avenue, not pursued in the present paper, is that heterogeneity in
27:935:68039:17:16:108:504:130:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:attention constraints may provoke multiple forms or degrees of attention manipula-
27:936:68121:16:0:108:503:114:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:tion.Banerjee and Mullainathan(2008) posit that the poor are subject to tighter
28:937:68202:0:17:108:504:673:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:attention constraints than the rich, who can afford better technologies to free up
28:938:68284:17:16:108:504:656:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:attention. They then show that this induces differences in productivity that amplify
28:939:68368:16:17:108:503:640:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:the differences in initial endowment; inequality breeds more inequality.Allcott and
28:940:68451:17:16:108:504:623:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:Taubinsky(2015)andTaubinsky and Rees-Jones(2015) similarly document consid-
28:941:68526:16:17:108:503:607:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:erable heterogeneity in attention limitations, andTaubinsky and Rees-Jones(2015)
28:942:68606:17:16:108:504:590:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:show that lower-income individuals have more severe attention limitations. The cur-
28:943:68689:16:17:108:504:574:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:rent paper’s findings suggest that the problem may be even worse: The poor may
28:944:68767:17:16:108:504:557:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:not only start out with tighter attention constraints, but may also find their limited
28:945:68853:16:16:108:504:541:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:attention exploited more than the rich. In short, the tighter constraints may make
28:946:68935:16:17:108:504:525:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:them less productiveand more manipulable. Manipulation is perhaps the more wor-
28:947:69014:17:16:108:504:508:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:risome problem in that it is, as shown in this paper, prone to create externalities,
28:948:69098:16:17:108:503:492:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:and thus constrained inefficient outcomes.  But such questions are left for future
28:949:69180:17:16:108:149:475:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:research.
28:950:69189:16:17:124:503:459:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:A:The poor may not only start out with tighter attention constraints, but may
28:951:69264:17:16:108:504:442:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:also find their limited attention exploited more than the rich. In short, the tighter
28:952:69349:16:16:108:508:426:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:constraints may make them less productiveand more manipulable.Manipulationis
28:953:69425:16:17:108:504:410:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:perhaps the more worrisome problem in that it is, as shown in this paper, prone to
28:954:69507:17:16:108:503:393:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:create externalities, and thus constrained inefficient outcomes. But such questions
28:955:69590:16:0:108:235:377:119:g_d0_f3:119:g_d0_f3:B:are left for future research.
